# React Native Skia Yoga Master Progress

Last updated: 2026-05-11

## Orchestrator State

- Active role: orchestrator.
- Goal state: active; do not mark complete.
- Product code changes authored by orchestrator: none; product changes are accepted worker patches only.
- Main worktree status at startup: clean on `main` tracking `origin/main`.
- Existing tmux sessions at startup: one unrelated `fast-react-*` session, left untouched.

## Pending Workers

## Decisions

- Keep orchestration documents inside the project repository so progress can be reviewed and merged.
- Start with read-only evidence gathering before assigning implementation work.
- Use separate git worktrees for top-level workers to avoid file conflicts.
- Top-level workers now run as managed Codex subagents launched with `spawn_agent`, not tmux subprocesses.
- Implementation workers use isolated git worktrees and branches. Launch them with `agent_type: "worker"`, `goal: true`, `fork_turns: "none"`, `model: "gpt-5.5"`, and `reasoning_effort: "xhigh"`.
- Worker prompts include the full task prompt, absolute worktree path, write scope, verification expectations, and overlap boundaries.
- `goal: true` replaces the former manual `create_goal`/`GOAL_CREATED` acceptance gate. Worker reports no longer need dedicated goal-lifecycle evidence.
- Workers may spawn nested managed subagents for hypothesis testing and must document delegated checks that affect their conclusions.
- Post-worker-102 target selection: worker 103 accepted worker 102's synthetic ImageCmd fit proof boundary, reconfirmed the 28-command feasible matrix, and selected bounded text/paragraph CSS color-string command conversion/render coverage as the strongest locally unblocked target because public JSX accepts string color values and native text-style conversion parses CSS strings while current text/paragraph command-render coverage uses numeric colors.
- Post-worker-106 target selection: worker 107 accepted worker 106's expanded generated `setCommand(...)` breadth, reconfirmed the 28-command feasible matrix, and selected direct `StrokeOpts` converter consistency as the strongest locally unblocked product-source target because `fromJSI(...)` rejects non-objects while `canConvert(...)` still advertises objects, `null`, and `undefined` as convertible.
- Post-worker-108 follow-up: direct `StrokeOpts` converter consistency is integrated; the next step is a fresh audit because worker 107's next-ranked TypeScript dynamic payload caveat needs API-boundary reassessment after the converter fix.
- Post-worker-109 target selection: worker 109 selected the public TypeScript dynamic command payload boundary and packed dynamic JSX proof because public JSX accepts broad `YogaDeepAnimated` command props, shipped source/spec payload types still expose some dynamic-capable leaves as plain numbers, and the packed TypeScript consumer verifier currently covers static JSX but not dynamic `SharedValue` command props.
- Post-worker-110 follow-up: packed dynamic JSX type-boundary proof is integrated; the next step is a fresh audit because worker 110 closed the public top-level TypeScript authoring proof while leaving deeper runtime/platform gaps intentionally out of scope.
- Post-worker-111 target selection: worker 111 selected package export-boundary hardening because worker 110 clarified the supported top-level authoring API but `package.json.files` still publishes `src`, no `exports` map constrains resolver entrypoints, and `src/specs/SkiaYoga.nitro.ts` still re-exports command transport types to deep importers.
- Post-worker-112 follow-up: package export-boundary hardening is integrated and the main 28-command feasible matrix passed; the next target is `JSIConverter<NodeCommand>::toJSI(...)` serialization symmetry, which worker 111 had ranked second after the package-boundary gap.
- Post-worker-113 follow-up: NodeCommand `toJSI(...)` serialization symmetry is integrated and the main 28-command feasible matrix passed; the next step is a fresh read-only root-cause audit because worker 111's ranked follow-ups are now closed or intentionally bounded.
- Post-worker-114 target selection: worker 114 selected materialized `YogaNode.getChildren()` return identity/prototype coverage because Reconciler cleanup recursively depends on `getChildren()`, native `YogaNode::getChildren()` currently returns children through `JSIConverter<std::shared_ptr<YogaNode>>::toJSI(...)`, and that converter creates a fresh plain NativeState object instead of the cached Nitro-materialized object/prototype.
- Post-worker-115 follow-up: materialized `YogaNode.getChildren()` identity/prototype behavior is integrated and the main 28-command feasible matrix passed; the next step is a fresh read-only root-cause audit because worker 115 closed the selected source/materialization boundary and the remaining gaps need reranking under the current proof surface.
- Post-worker-116 target selection: worker 116 selected whole `SharedValue<SamplingOptions>` public type support for `image.sampling` because `SamplingOptions` is opaque but union-shaped, `YogaDeepAnimated<T>` currently distributes over that union, and the public type rejects `SharedValue<SamplingOptions>` while accepting narrower `SharedValue<FilterOptions>` / `SharedValue<CubicResampler>`.
- Worker 117 accepted that target within a TypeScript/package/source-level proof boundary. Whole `SharedValue<SamplingOptions>` now compiles for `image.sampling` from an installed tarball, nested sampling leaves remain rejected, Reconciler JS listener coverage includes top-level opaque `image.sampling`, and the main 28-command feasible matrix passed. The next step is a fresh post-worker-117 audit.
- Worker 118 accepted the post-worker-117 baseline, reconfirmed the 28-command feasible matrix, and selected bounded value-bearing `toJSI(...)` serialization for `SkSamplingOptions`, `TextStyle`, and `ParagraphStyle` because those converters parse meaningful JS payloads but still serialize empty objects.
- Worker 119 closed the selected serialization target for bounded stable fields and reconfirmed the main 28-command feasible matrix. Remaining style/sampling risks are unsupported `maxAniso`, un-serialized text/paragraph fields, CSS string preservation, exact typography/shaping/render fidelity, and platform/runtime proof gaps.
- Worker 120 accepted the post-worker-119 proof boundary and selected canonical `style.antiAlias` support because the public/generated/native contract currently exposes the misspelled `antiaAlias`, while Skia/RN Skia spelling and expected authoring use `antiAlias`.
- Worker 121 closed canonical `style.antiAlias` support within a public TypeScript/generated/native/host-SkPaint proof boundary, preserved deprecated `style.antiaAlias` fallback with canonical precedence, and reconfirmed the main 28-command feasible matrix. The next step is a fresh post-worker-121 audit.
- Worker 122 accepted worker 121's boundary, reconfirmed the main 28-command feasible matrix, and selected bounded additional `TextStyle` `toJSI(...)` serialization because the native converter parses meaningful public fields that current serialization still drops.
- Worker 123 closed the selected `TextStyle` serialization target for background/foreground colors, decoration fields, font style, shadows, and text baseline, and reconfirmed the main 28-command feasible matrix. The next step is a fresh post-worker-123 audit.
- Worker 124 accepted worker 123's boundary, reconfirmed the main 28-command feasible matrix, and selected bounded `TextStyle.fontFeatures` `toJSI(...)` serialization because it remains a public-shaped field parsed by `fromJSI(...)` but dropped by `toJSI(...)`.
- Worker 125 closed the selected `TextStyle.fontFeatures` serialization target, added direct and representative command round-trip proof, and reconfirmed the main 28-command feasible matrix. The next step is a fresh post-worker-125 audit.

## Evidence Summary

- JS/API: package metadata and JSX runtime declarations originally pointed at missing `lib` output; worker 005 aligned the source-first entrypoints and JSX runtime declarations. Worker 031 closed the remaining README/API contract drift by documenting peer dependencies, documenting the `jsxImportSource: "react-native-skia-yoga"` TypeScript setup required for lowercase intrinsic-node usage, and correcting stale Nitro public package metadata URLs. The unsupported public `origin` field and overly broad nested animated style typing were addressed by worker 009.
- Native reset semantics: optional native style and command prop omission now resets to defaults instead of preserving stale native state. Worker 008 also preserves the text fallback color contract: `backgroundColor` wins, explicit `opacity` controls alpha, and fallback text alpha is preserved when opacity is omitted.
- Native: platform context ownership was unified by worker 006. Raw `_parent` pointers in `YogaNode` were replaced by weak parent links by worker 011, and child reparenting now enforces a single-parent invariant with exact interactive-descendant count updates.
- Verification: worker 004 fixed the root/example install-isolation bug that let `scripts/sync-example-links.mjs` clobber root dependency/bin/type resolution. `bun run check:install-isolation` now guards that boundary. Worker 012 added `bun run check:yoganode-native-lifetime`, a focused syntax/source-invariant verifier for the YogaNode weak-parent and reparenting invariants. Worker 013 added `bun run check:yoganode-native-runtime`, a linked host-native runtime smoke that executes retained-descendant teardown and reparenting ownership assertions. Worker 021 restored that runtime smoke for the current RN Skia macOS packaging by preferring optional/current xcframework layouts, validating the expected archive basenames, and retaining legacy `libs/macos` discovery as fallback. Worker 022 confirmed the currently feasible main checks pass and selected Android RN Skia archive discovery as the next unblocked native-build feedback-loop target. Worker 023 fixed that Android archive discovery path in `android/CMakeLists.txt` and added `check:android-skia-archives` to guard the current optional-package Android archive layout and exact CMake candidate-list ordering. Worker 024 confirmed those package/native checks remain green and selected `lint-ci` repair as the next unblocked repo-owned feedback-loop target. Worker 025 repaired root lint-ci by adding an explicit root ESLint config, fixing React Native lint dependency resolution, replacing the missing CI formatter with installed/default formatter wiring, and preserving source/example/script lint scope. Worker 026 confirmed `lint-ci` now passes with warnings and selected the two product-source React Native deep imports as the next unblocked repo-owned cleanup. Worker 027 completed that cleanup, leaving `lint-ci` passing with only the 178 example/demo warning backlog. Worker 028 confirmed the rest of the feasible verification matrix remains green and selected example lint-contract cleanup as the next repo-owned feedback-loop target. Worker 029 completed that cleanup, and `npm run lint-ci` now passes with 0 warnings and 0 errors. Worker 030 confirmed the feasible checks remain green after lint cleanup and selected README/API documentation drift as the next repo-owned contract target. Worker 031 completed that target and main verification remains green, including bounded package lifecycle verification. Worker 032 found that current package checks still miss native publish-surface completeness because `cpp/` is absent from the packed manifest despite being required by native build metadata. Worker 033 fixed that gap and added `check:package-surface`, which now verifies the actual pack manifest includes all shared `cpp/` files, key iOS/Android/Nitrogen/package files, and the Android `fix-prefab.gradle` helper required by `android/build.gradle`. Worker 034 confirmed those checks remain green and selected the unguarded example Expo export path plus Metro config dump as the next feedback-loop hygiene target. Worker 035 added `check:example-bundle`, so the feasible matrix now includes a repo-owned bounded Expo iOS export smoke that cleans temporary output and no longer emits the Metro config dump. Worker 036 confirmed the full feasible matrix remains green and selected RN Skia private import cleanup because `src/YogaCanvas.tsx` still depended on private RN Skia native-ID internals with Node resolution failure evidence. Worker 037 completed that cleanup and added `check:rn-skia-imports`, which guards tracked source against RN Skia `src/`, `lib/typescript/src/`, and private `SkiaViewNativeId` deep imports. Worker 038 confirmed that the feasible matrix remains green after worker 037 and selected packed-package TypeScript consumer smoke coverage because no current verifier compiles public entrypoints and lowercase JSX from an installed package tarball. Worker 039 added that verifier as `check:package-typescript-consumer`, proving a packed tarball can be installed into a temporary external TypeScript consumer and compile public entrypoints plus lowercase intrinsic JSX under `jsxImportSource: "react-native-skia-yoga"`. Worker 040 confirmed the verifier is meaningful but depended on a consumer-side `@types/react-reconciler` workaround; a scratch packed-consumer probe without that type package failed with TS7016 from `src/Reconciler.ts`, making package-surface dependency hygiene the next strongest unblocked target. Worker 041 completed that target by publishing direct `react-reconciler` and `@types/react-reconciler` dependencies and updating `check:package-typescript-consumer` so the temporary consumer no longer declares `@types/react-reconciler` while the packed package asserts and prints both reconciler dependencies. Worker 042 confirmed dependency hygiene is now closed with the full feasible matrix green and selected public declaration/export boundary cleanup because top-level declarations still re-export `./src/index`, `src/index.ts` still exports implementation internals such as `./Reconciler`, and `src/SkiaYogaObject.ts` remains import-time side-effectful. Worker 043 completed that boundary cleanup by replacing top-level wildcard exports with explicit allowlists, keeping source-first runtime files packed intentionally, and strengthening `check:package-surface` plus `check:package-typescript-consumer` so public packed-consumer usage is guarded while internal top-level names are rejected. Worker 045 added `check:skia-yoga-object-lazy-init`, which now proves import-only public source access does not perform `SkiaYoga` native lookup/install/hybrid creation, initialization logging, or `globalThis.SkiaYoga` mutation, while explicit native access initializes exactly once. Worker 046 confirmed worker 045's target is closed, documented that the verifier intentionally stubs `src/util.ts`, and selected broader public import-only Nitro side-effect coverage around `src/util.ts` as the next unblocked verification-backed implementation target. Worker 047 closed that target by moving `src/util.ts` Nitro boxing behind a lazy cached accessor, removing the verifier's `src/util.ts` public-import stub, and proving public import-only paths stay free of Nitro boxing/unboxing and native/global side effects while explicit `createYogaNode()` and `YogaCanvas` root creation still create YogaNode hybrid objects lazily. Worker 048 confirmed the full feasible matrix remains green, verified the remaining lazy Nitro risk is Worklets transform/closure coverage rather than public import-time side effects, and selected a focused `src/util.ts` Worklets transform/closure guard as the next unblocked verification target. Worker 049 added that transform guard to `check:skia-yoga-object-lazy-init`, making the verifier fail if transformed `createYogaNode()` loses `lazyNitroModulesBox`, directly captures `NitroModules`, adds bypass captures, or loses the `lazyNitroModulesBox.current.unbox()` worklet body path. Worker 050 confirmed worker 049's guard is meaningful root transform-level proof, documented that it is not device/UI-runtime Worklets proof, and selected an example/Expo Babel-config Worklets guard for the package source path as the next unblocked verification target. Worker 052 confirmed worker 051 closed that transform/config gap and selected public-import verifier hardening around the real import graph and native component registration as the next unblocked verification target. Worker 053 completed that hardening by loading the real project-side public import graph in `check:skia-yoga-object-lazy-init`, counting the expected SkiaYogaView native component registration, and keeping `NativeSkiaYoga` runtime lookup outside the supported public import graph. Worker 054 accepted that proof boundary and selected direct `src/specs/NativeSkiaYoga.ts` deep-import hardening as the next strongest repo-owned import-time native lookup target. Worker 055 completed that hardening by deferring the direct `NativeSkiaYoga` TurboModule lookup until explicit `install()` while preserving codegen parser compatibility and adding direct deep-import lazy coverage to `check:skia-yoga-object-lazy-init`. Worker 056 accepted that boundary and selected automation of the manual RN codegen parser/schema proof as the next unblocked package/native contract target. Worker 057 completed that target with `check:rn-codegen-schema`, which ties local React Native parser/schema proof to `package.json.codegenConfig`, asserts the current NativeModule/component schema, and documents intentionally ignored non-RN-codegen files under `src/specs`. Worker 058 accepted that boundary after repaired example-check evidence and selected broader Worklets transform verification for `src/Reconciler.ts` and `src/useCanvasGestures.ts` as the next unblocked transform-level target. Worker 059 completed that target by adding root and example Babel/Expo transform assertions for Reconciler animated binding worklets and YogaCanvas gesture callback worklets to `check:skia-yoga-object-lazy-init`, while documenting that the proof remains transform/closure-level only.
- Runtime verifier gaps: worker 060 accepted worker 059 within the transform/closure proof boundary and selected source-level Reconciler animated binding state-transition verification as the next strongest unblocked target. Worker 061 completed that target with `check:reconciler-animated-bindings`, proving local source-level host-config transitions with stubs and without claiming real UI-runtime/native proof. Worker 062 completed the next local runtime gap with `check:gesture-interaction-runtime`, proving `YogaInteractionRegistry` and `useCanvasGestures` source-level state transitions, event payloads, dispatch ordering, cleanup, cancellation, failure paths, and selected `YogaCanvas` wiring with local stubs only. Worker 063 accepted those boundaries and selected the remaining `YogaCanvas` lifecycle/render/profiling source-level runtime gap. Worker 064 completed that target with `check:yogacanvas-lifecycle-runtime`, proving local source-level YogaCanvas lifecycle, render retry, animation, profiling, and unmount cleanup behavior with stubs while not claiming real native/UI-runtime proof.
- Package/native consumer feedback: worker 065 confirmed the remaining high-value unblocked gap was installed-tarball React Native codegen/autolinking proof. Worker 066 closed that gap with `check:package-codegen-autolinking`, which packs and installs the tarball into an external temporary React Native consumer, proves the installed package is non-symlinked and outside the repo, runs RN codegen against installed package specs, asserts the expected schema/files, and verifies iOS/Android React Native CLI autolinking metadata from the installed package path. ## Known Hygiene Notes

- Do not delete or modify unrelated `fr-*`, `fast-react-*`, or `spacebar-*` tmux sessions.
- `node_modules/` exists in the main worktree and should not be treated as a worker artifact.
- Ignored local `example/ios/` and `example/android/` directories exist in the main checkout. They are not tracked and were left untouched.
- Ignored local `example/.expo/` exists in the main checkout with timestamps predating worker 037 verification. It is not tracked and was left untouched as ambiguous local state.
- `tsconfig.tsbuildinfo` exists in the main worktree before orchestration; do not remove it without explicit evidence it is generated noise owned by this project state.
